__bootstrap:
	NEW_SCOPE
	BEGIN_STRUCT dpu_set_t
	APPEND_INT 0 foo
	END_STRUCT
	BEGIN_STRUCT dpu_arguments_t
	APPEND_INT 0 size
	APPEND_INT 0 transfer_size
	APPEND_INT 0 kernel
	END_STRUCT
	NEW_GLOBAL_INT 0 NUM_DPUS
	GET_IDENTIFIER NUM_DPUS
	PUSH_INT 512
	ASSIGN
	NEW_GLOBAL_INT 0 NUM_TASKLETS
	GET_IDENTIFIER NUM_TASKLETS
	PUSH_INT 16
	ASSIGN
	NEW_GLOBAL_INT 0 DATA_PREP_PARAMS
	GET_IDENTIFIER DATA_PREP_PARAMS
	PUSH_INT 2097152
	ASSIGN
	CALL main
	DELETE_SCOPE
read_input:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 i
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	PUSH_INT 0
	ASSIGN
	JUMP L0
L0:
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_NONZERO L1
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_ZERO L2
L1:
	NEW_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER A
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	ASSIGN
	GET_IDENTIFIER B
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	ASSIGN
	DELETE_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	ASSIGN_PLUS_PLUS
	JUMP L0
L2:
	DELETE_SCOPE
	DELETE_SCOPE
vector_addition_host:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 i
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	PUSH_INT 0
	ASSIGN
	JUMP L3
L3:
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_NONZERO L4
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_ZERO L5
L4:
	NEW_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER C
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	GET_IDENTIFIER A
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	GET_IDENTIFIER B
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	ADD
	ASSIGN
	DELETE_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	ASSIGN_PLUS_PLUS
	JUMP L3
L5:
	DELETE_SCOPE
	DELETE_SCOPE
roundup:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_RETURN_INT 0
	GET_IDENTIFIER n
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	DIV
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	MUL
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	ADD
	ASSIGN_RETURN
	RETURN
	DELETE_SCOPE
divceil:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_RETURN_INT 0
	GET_IDENTIFIER n
	PUSH_INT 1
	SUB
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	DIV
	PUSH_INT 1
	ADD
	ASSIGN_RETURN
	RETURN
	DELETE_SCOPE
main:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 BL
	GET_IDENTIFIER BL
	PUSH_INT 10
	ASSIGN
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 BLOCK_SIZE_LOG2
	GET_IDENTIFIER BLOCK_SIZE_LOG2
	GET_IDENTIFIER BL
	ASSIGN
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 BLOCK_SIZE
	GET_IDENTIFIER BLOCK_SIZE
	PUSH_INT 1
	GET_IDENTIFIER BLOCK_SIZE_LOG2
	LSHIFT
	ASSIGN
	NEW_FAST_INT 1 A
	NEW_FAST_INT 1 B
	NEW_FAST_INT 1 C
	NEW_FAST_INT 1 C2
	NEW_FAST_STRUCT 0 dpu_set_t dpu_set
	NEW_FAST_STRUCT 0 dpu_set_t dpu
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 nr_of_dpus
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_of_dpus
	GET_IDENTIFIER NUM_DPUS
	ASSIGN
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 input_size
	GET_IDENTIFIER input_size
	GET_IDENTIFIER DATA_PREP_PARAMS
	ASSIGN
	DPU_ALLOC 0
	DPU_ALLOC 1
	DPU_ALLOC 2
	DPU_ALLOC 3
